 mayawati ke bare main reeta bahuguna joshi ne kuch apshabd kahe the jiske baad bispi ke kaaryakartaaon ne reeta bahuguna joshi ke ghar aag laga di thi
 Evergreen Jacques Kallis's unbeaten century and two back-to-back strikes at the start made India come back well on the second day of the third and final Test cricket match against South Africa through the vigilant innings of openers Gautam Gambhir and Sachin Tendulkar
 kallis ne ankar kii bhoomika nibhaakar apana 39waan shatak jadaa
 He scored 161 runs before being dismissed as the last batsman, leading South Africa to a challenging score of 362
 bharat ne iske baad 28 ran par do wicket ganvaa die the, lekin gambhir (naabad 65) or tendulkar (naabad 49) ke bich tisare wicket ke liye 39 over main 114 ran kii atoot saajhedaari se vah duusare din kaa khel samaapt hone tak do wicket par 142 ran tak pahunchane main safal rahaa
 India is still 220 runs behind South Africa
 dakshin africa ke aath wicket par 283 ran par ukhd gaye the or uskaa 300 ran tak pahunchnaa bhi mushkil lag rahaa tha, lekin kallis ne aakhir ke do ballebaaj paul haris (7) or lonawabo sotsobe (naabad 8) ke saath 79 ran jodakar team ko achche score tak pahunchaaya
 For India, Sreesanth took five for 114, Zaheer Khan three for 89 and Ishant Sharma took two wickets for 77 runs
 bharat kii shuruyaat acchhee nahin rahi tathaa del sten ne virendra sahvaag (13) ke aakraamak tevar jald hi thande kar die
 Rahul Dravid (5) also returned to the pavilion after being run out, but Gambhir, who got two lives and survived two reliable appeals from Pagbadha, did not allow India to suffer further blows
 dravid ne satark ravaiya apanaaya, lekin vidambnaa rahi ki jis gend par gambhir kaa kaich chhot gaya tha, us par vah ran out ho gaye
 Alviro Peterson dropped Gambhir in the lane off Sotsobe, but AB de Villiers fielding at slip, caught the ball and sent Dravid to the pavilion, throwing a wicket at the striker's end
 gambhir iske baad jab 60 ran par the, tab sotsobe kii hi gend par divilliars ne slip main unka kaich choda
 Tendulkar instinctively moved his innings forward
 is bich unhone morkal ke ek over main do chauke jadkar team par se dabaav hataane kii koshish kii
 Paul Harris made a reliable appeal of lbw against him in the 26th over, but was turned down by Simon Tuffel
 riple se haalanki tab lag rahaa tha ki gend leg stump par lagati
 Gambhir then completed his 15th half-century in the next over, hitting a four at midwicket at Sotsobe
